QUANTD(2 years,2)
QUANTD(2 days,2)
VDOMAIN_MODAL(be,will)
SUBJ_PRE(will,It)
NUCL_VLINK_MODAL(will,be)
SUBJ-N_PRE(be,It)
PREPD(days,in)
MAIN_MODAL(be)
HEAD(2 years,2 years)
HEAD(2 days,2 days)
HEAD(in 2 days,in 2 days)
HEAD(It,It)
TEMPEXPR(exactly 2 years ago)
TEMPEXPR(2 years ago)
TEMPEXPR(ago)
TEMP_POST(be,in 2 days)
TEMP_POST_T_RELAT(be,exactly 2 years ago)
TIMEX3(2 years)
TIMEX3(in 2 days)
TIMEX3_T_RELAT(exactly 2 years ago)

VASPECT_A_SIMPLE(be)
FUTURE(be)
ST-ORDER_TEMP_REL(be)
